      (fc2): Conv1d(256, 256, kernel_size=(1,), stride=(1,))

      (predictor): Conv1d(256, 2, kernel_size=(1,), stride=(1,))
    )
    (dice_loss): DiceLoss()
    (focal_loss): FocalLoss()
  )
)

      (batch_norm1): BatchNorm2d(256, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1, affine=True, track_running_stats=True)

    (linear_layer): Linear(in_features=5120, out_features=32768, bias=True)
    (point_head): StandardPointHead(
      (coef): Conv2d(256, 256, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1))
      (freq): Conv2d(256, 256, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1))
      (phase): Linear(in_features=2, out_features=128, bias=False)
      (imnet): MLP(
        (layers): Sequential(
          (0): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=True)
          (1): ReLU()
          (2): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=True)
          (3): ReLU()
          (4): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=True)
          (5): ReLU()
          (6): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=2, bias=True)
        )
      )
      (fc1): Conv1d(256, 256, kernel_size=(1,), stride=(1,))
      (fc2): Conv1d(256, 256, kernel_size=(1,), stride=(1,))
      (fc3): Conv1d(256, 256, kernel_size=(1,), stride=(1,))
      (predictor): Conv1d(256, 2, kernel_size=(1,), stride=(1,))
    )
    (dice_loss): DiceLoss()
    (focal_loss): FocalLoss()
  )
)
